<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">第一<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>第一</rb><rt>だいいち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;1st</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">夜<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>夜</rb><rt>や</rt></ruby>&nbsp;night</span></span></p><br/>

<p>こんな<span class="vocab" onclick="">夢<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>夢</rb><rt>ゆめ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;dream</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">見た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;saw; had (a dream)</span></span></p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">腕組をして<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>腕組</rb><rt>うでぐみ</rt></ruby>をして&nbsp;fold one's arms in front of one</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">枕元<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>枕元</rb><rt>まくらもと</rt></ruby>&nbsp;by (someone's) pillow; (resting) on one's back</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">寝た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>寝</rb><rt>ね</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;be resting; be lying down</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">女<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>女</rb><rt>おんな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;woman</span></span>が、<span class="vocab" onclick="">静かな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>静</rb><rt>しず</rt></ruby>かな&nbsp;quiet; soft (voice)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">声<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>声</rb><rt>こえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;voice</span></span>でもう<span class="vocab" onclick="">死にます<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>死</rb><rt>し</rt></ruby>にます&nbsp;die; pass away</span></span>と<span class="vocab" onclick="">云う<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>う&nbsp;said</span></span>。女は<span class="vocab" onclick="">長い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>長</rb><rt>なが</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;long</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">髪<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>髪</rb><rt>かみ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hair</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">枕<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>枕</rb><rt>まくら</rt></ruby>&nbsp;pillow</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">敷いて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>敷</rb><rt>し</rt></ruby>いて&nbsp;spread</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">輪郭<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>輪郭</rb><rt>りんかく</rt></ruby>&nbsp;outline; contour</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">柔らかな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>柔</rb><rt>やわ</rt></ruby>らかな&nbsp;soft; tender</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">瓜実顔<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>瓜実</rb><rt>うりざね</rt></ruby><ruby><rb>顔</rb><rt>がお</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oval face</span></span>をその<span class="vocab" onclick="">中<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>中</rb><rt>なか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;middle; midst</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">横たえて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>横</rb><rt>よこ</rt></ruby>たえて&nbsp;lay down (on)</span></span>いる。<span class="vocab" onclick="">真白な<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>真白</rb><rt>まっしろ</rt></ruby>な&nbsp;pure white</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">頬<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>頬</rb><rt>ほお</rt></ruby>&nbsp;cheeks</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">底<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>底</rb><rt>そこ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;depths</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">温かい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>温</rb><rt>あたた</rt></ruby>かい&nbsp;warm</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">血<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>血</rb><rt>ち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;blood</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">色<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>色</rb><rt>いろ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;color</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">ほどよく<span class="vocabdef">ほどよく&nbsp;moderately; to just the proper degree</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">差して<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>差</rb><rt>さ</rt></ruby>して&nbsp;tinge; flush (with color)</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">唇<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>唇</rb><rt>くちびる</rt></ruby>&nbsp;lips</span></span>の色は<span class="vocab" onclick="">無論<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>無論</rb><rt>むろん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;(as a matter) of course</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">赤い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>赤</rb><rt>あか</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;red</span></span>。とうてい死にそうには<span class="vocab" onclick="">見えない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>えない&nbsp;didn't appear (to be ...)</span></span>。しかし女は静かな声で、もう死にますと<span class="vocab" onclick="">判然<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>判然</rb><rt>はっきり</rt></ruby>&nbsp;clearly</span></span>云った。<span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>も<span class="vocab" onclick="">確に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>確</rb><rt>たしか</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;assuredly; without doubt</span></span>これは死ぬなと思った。そこで、そうかね、もう死ぬのかね、と<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;above</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">覗き込む<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>覗</rb><rt>のぞ</rt></ruby>き<ruby><rb>込</rb><rt>こ</rt></ruby>む&nbsp;look into (someone's face)</span></span>ようにして<span class="vocab" onclick="">聞いて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>聞</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>いて&nbsp;ask; inquire</span></span>見た。死にますとも、と云いながら、女は<span class="vocab" onclick="">ぱっちりと<span class="vocabdef">ぱっちりと&nbsp;widely; brightly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">眼<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眼</rb><rt>め</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eyes</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">開けた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>開</rb><rt>あ</rt></ruby>けた&nbsp;opened</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">大きな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>大</rb><rt>おお</rt></ruby>きな&nbsp;large</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">潤<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>潤</rb><rt>うるおい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;moisture; dampness</span></span>のある眼で、長い<span class="vocab" onclick="">睫<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>睫</rb><rt>まつげ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eyelashes; lashes</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">包まれた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>包</rb><rt>つつ</rt></ruby>まれた&nbsp;be wrapped (in)</span></span>中は、ただ<span class="vocab" onclick="">一面に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>一面</rb><rt>いちめん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;all over (a single surface)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">真黒<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>真黒</rb><rt>まっくろ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;pitch black</span></span>であった。その真黒な<span class="vocab" onclick="">眸<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眸</rb><rt>ひとみ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;pupils</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">奥<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>奥</rb><rt>おく</rt></ruby>&nbsp;interior; depths</span></span>に、自分の<span class="vocab" onclick="">姿<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>姿</rb><rt>すがた</rt></ruby>&nbsp;shape; form</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">鮮に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鮮</rb><rt>あざやか</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;clearly; distinctly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">浮かんで<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>浮</rb><rt>う</rt></ruby>かんで&nbsp;float; be reflected</span></span>いる。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">透き徹る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>透</rb><rt>す</rt></ruby>き<ruby><rb>徹</rb><rt>とお</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;be transparent</span></span>ほど<span class="vocab" onclick="">深く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>深</rb><rt>ふか</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;deep</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">見える<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>える&nbsp;appear</span></span>この<span class="vocab" onclick="">黒眼<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>黒眼</rb><rt>くろめ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;black eyes; ebony eyes</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">色沢<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>色沢</rb><rt>つや</rt></ruby>&nbsp;gloss; luster</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">眺めて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眺</rb><rt>なが</rt></ruby>めて&nbsp;gaze (at)</span></span>、これでも<span class="vocab" onclick="">死ぬ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>死</rb><rt>し</rt></ruby>ぬ&nbsp;die; pass away</span></span>のかと<span class="vocab" onclick="">思った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;wondered</span></span>。それで、<span class="vocab" onclick="">ねんごろに<span class="vocabdef">ねんごろに&nbsp;carefully</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">枕<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>枕</rb><rt>まくら</rt></ruby>&nbsp;pillow</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">傍<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>傍</rb><rt>そば</rt></ruby>&nbsp;side; proximity</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">口<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>口</rb><rt>くち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;mouth</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">付けて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>付</rb><rt>つ</rt></ruby>けて&nbsp;brought near (to); positioned</span></span>、死ぬんじゃなかろうね、<span class="vocab" onclick="">大丈夫<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>大丈夫</rb><rt>だいじょうぶ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;safe; secure; all right</span></span>だろうね、とまた<span class="vocab" onclick="">聞き返した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>聞</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>き<ruby><rb>返</rb><rt>かえ</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;asked again</span></span>。すると<span class="vocab" onclick="">女<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>女</rb><rt>おんな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;woman</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">黒い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>黒</rb><rt>くろ</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;black; ebony</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">眼<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眼</rb><rt>め</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eyes</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">眠そうに<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眠</rb><rt>ねむ</rt></ruby>そうに&nbsp;in a weary manner</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">睜た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>睜</rb><rt>みはっ</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;opened wide (eyes)</span></span>まま、やっぱり<span class="vocab" onclick="">静かな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>静</rb><rt>しず</rt></ruby>かな&nbsp;quiet; soft (voice)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">声<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>声</rb><rt>こえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;voice</span></span>で、でも、死ぬんですもの、<span class="vocab" onclick="">仕方がない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>仕方</rb><rt>しかた</rt></ruby>がない&nbsp;can't be avoided</span></span>わと<span class="vocab" onclick="">云った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;said</span></span>。</p>

<p>じゃ、<span class="vocab" onclick="">私の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>私</rb><rt>わたし</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;my</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">顔<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>顔</rb><rt>かお</rt></ruby>&nbsp;face</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">見える<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>える&nbsp;be visible</span></span>かいと<span class="vocab" onclick="">一心に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>一心</rb><rt>いっしん</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;intently; earnestly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">聞く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>聞</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;ask; inquire</span></span>と、見えるかいって、そら、そこに、<span class="vocab" onclick="">写って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>写</rb><rt>うつ</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;be reflected</span></span>るじゃありませんかと、<span class="vocab" onclick="">にこりと笑って<span class="vocabdef">にこりと<ruby><rb>笑</rb><rt>わら</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;smile gently; break into a smile</span></span>見せた。<span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">黙って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>黙</rb><rt>だま</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;remain silent</span></span>、顔を<span class="vocab" onclick="">枕<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>枕</rb><rt>まくら</rt></ruby>&nbsp;pillow</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">離した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>離</rb><rt>はな</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;separated from; withdrew</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">腕組をしながら<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>腕組</rb><rt>うでぐみ</rt></ruby>をしながら&nbsp;folding one's arms in front of one</span></span>、どうしても<span class="vocab" onclick="">死ぬ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>死</rb><rt>し</rt></ruby>ぬ&nbsp;die; pass away</span></span>のかなと<span class="vocab" onclick="">思った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;wondered</span></span>。</p>

<p>しばらくして、<span class="vocab" onclick="">女<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>女</rb><rt>おんな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;woman</span></span>がまたこう<span class="vocab" onclick="">云った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;said</span></span>。</p>

<p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">死んだら<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>死</rb><rt>し</rt></ruby>んだら&nbsp;when (I) die</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">埋めて下さい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>埋</rb><rt>う</rt></ruby>めて<ruby><rb>下</rb><rt>くだ</rt></ruby>さい&nbsp;please bury (me)</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">大きな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>大</rb><rt>おお</rt></ruby>きな&nbsp;large</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">真珠貝<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>真珠貝</rb><rt>しんじゅがい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;pearl oyster shell</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">穴<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>穴</rb><rt>あな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hole</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">掘って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>掘</rb><rt>ほ</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;dig</span></span>。そうして<span class="vocab" onclick="">天<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>天</rb><rt>てん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;the heavens</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">落ちて来る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>落</rb><rt>お</rt></ruby>ちて<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>く</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;fall down; come falling</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">星<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>星</rb><rt>ほし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;star</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">破片<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>破片</rb><rt>かけ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;splinter; fragment</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">墓標<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>墓標</rb><rt>はかじるし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;grave marker</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">置いて下さい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>置</rb><rt>お</rt></ruby>いて<ruby><rb>下</rb><rt>くだ</rt></ruby>さい&nbsp;please place</span></span>。そうして墓の<span class="vocab" onclick="">傍<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>傍</rb><rt>そば</rt></ruby>&nbsp;side; vicinity</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">待って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>待</rb><rt>ま</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;wait</span></span>いて下さい。また<span class="vocab" onclick="">逢いに来ます<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>逢</rb><rt>あ</rt></ruby>いに<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>ます&nbsp;come to see (a person)</span></span>から」</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>は、いつ<span class="vocab" onclick="">逢いに来る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>逢</rb><rt>あ</rt></ruby>いに<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>く</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;come to see (a person)</span></span>かねと<span class="vocab" onclick="">聞いた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>聞</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>いた&nbsp;asked</span></span>。</p>

<p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">日が出る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>日</rb><rt>ひ</rt></ruby>が<ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>で</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;the sun will rise</span></span>でしょう。それから<span class="vocab" onclick="">日が沈む<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>日</rb><rt>ひ</rt></ruby>が<ruby><rb>沈</rb><rt>しず</rt></ruby>む&nbsp;the sun will set</span></span>でしょう。それからまた出るでしょう、そうしてまた沈むでしょう。――<span class="vocab" onclick="">赤い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>赤</rb><rt>あか</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;red</span></span>日が<span class="vocab" onclick="">東<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>東</rb><rt>ひがし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;east</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">西<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>西</rb><rt>にし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;west</span></span>へ、東から西へと<span class="vocab" onclick="">落ちて行く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>落</rb><rt>お</rt></ruby>ちて<ruby><rb>行</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;go down</span></span>うちに、――あなた、<span class="vocab" onclick="">待って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>待</rb><rt>ま</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;wait</span></span>いられますか」</p>

<p>自分は<span class="vocab" onclick="">黙って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>黙</rb><rt>だま</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;remaining silent</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">首肯いた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>首肯</rb><rt>うなず</rt></ruby>いた&nbsp;nodded assent</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">女<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>女</rb><rt>おんな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;woman</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">静かな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>静</rb><rt>しず</rt></ruby>かな&nbsp;quiet</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">調子<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>調子</rb><rt>ちょうし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tone (of voice)</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">一段<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>一段</rb><rt>いちだん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;one step; one stage</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">張り上げて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>張</rb><rt>は</rt></ruby>り<ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>あ</rt></ruby>げて&nbsp;raise; lift up (one's voice)</span></span>、</p>

<p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">百年<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>百年</rb><rt>ひゃくねん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;a hundred years</span></span>待っていて下さい」と<span class="vocab" onclick="">思い切った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>い<ruby><rb>切</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;resolute; decisive</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">声<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>声</rb><rt>こえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;voice</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">云った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;said</span></span>。</p>

<p>「百年、<span class="vocab" onclick="">私の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>私</rb><rt>わたし</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;my</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">墓<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>墓</rb><rt>はか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;grave</span></span>の傍に<span class="vocab" onclick="">坐って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>坐</rb><rt>すわ</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;sit</span></span>待っていて下さい。きっと逢いに来ますから」</p>

<p>自分はただ待っていると<span class="vocab" onclick="">答えた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>答</rb><rt>こた</rt></ruby>えた&nbsp;answered</span></span>。すると、<span class="vocab" onclick="">黒い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>黒</rb><rt>くろ</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;black; distinctly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">見えた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>えた&nbsp;was visible</span></span>自分の<span class="vocab" onclick="">姿<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>姿</rb><rt>すがた</rt></ruby>&nbsp;shape; form</span></span>が、ぼうっと<span class="vocab" onclick="">崩れて来た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>崩</rb><rt>くず</rt></ruby>れて<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;broke apart; disintegrated</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">静かな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>静</rb><rt>しず</rt></ruby>かな&nbsp;still; quiet</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">水<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>水</rb><rt>みず</rt></ruby>&nbsp;water</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">動いて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>動</rb><rt>うご</rt></ruby>いて&nbsp;move</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">写る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>写</rb><rt>うつ</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;be reflected</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">影<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>影</rb><rt>かげ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;form; image</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">乱した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>乱</rb><rt>みだ</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;stirred; disrupted</span></span>ように、<span class="vocab" onclick="">流れ出した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>流</rb><rt>なが</rt></ruby>れ<ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>だ</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;began to flow</span></span>と思ったら、女の<span class="vocab" onclick="">眼<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眼</rb><rt>め</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eyes</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">ぱちりと<span class="vocabdef">ぱちりと&nbsp;like a shutter</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">閉じた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>閉</rb><rt>と</rt></ruby>じた&nbsp;closed</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">長い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>長</rb><rt>なが</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;long</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">睫<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>睫</rb><rt>まつげ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eyelashes; lashes</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">間<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>間</rb><rt>あいだ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;midst</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">涙<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>涙</rb><rt>なみだ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tear</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">頬<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>頬</rb><rt>ほお</rt></ruby>&nbsp;cheek</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">垂れた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>垂</rb><rt>た</rt></ruby>れた&nbsp;dropped (onto)</span></span>。――もう<span class="vocab" onclick="">死んでいた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>死</rb><rt>し</rt></ruby>んでいた&nbsp;be dead; be gone</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>はそれから<span class="vocab" onclick="">庭<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>庭</rb><rt>にわ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;garden; earth</span></span>をすくうたびに、貝の<span class="vocab" onclick="">裏<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>裏</rb><rt>うら</rt></ruby>&nbsp;reverse; back side</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">月<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>月</rb><rt>つき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;moon</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">光<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>光</rb><rt>ひかり</rt></ruby>&nbsp;light; (moon) beams</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">差して<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>差</rb><rt>さ</rt></ruby>して&nbsp;shine (on); strike</span></span>きらきらした。<span class="vocab" onclick="">湿った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>湿</rb><rt>しめ</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;moist</span></span>土の<span class="vocab" onclick="">匂<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>匂</rb><rt>におい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;smell</span></span>もした。穴はしばらくして掘れた。<span class="vocab" onclick="">女<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>女</rb><rt>おんな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;woman</span></span>をその<span class="vocab" onclick="">中<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>中</rb><rt>なか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;middle</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">入れた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>入</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>れた&nbsp;put into</span></span>。そうして<span class="vocab" onclick="">柔らかい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>柔</rb><rt>やわ</rt></ruby>らかい&nbsp;soft</span></span>土を、<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;above</span></span>からそっと<span class="vocab" onclick="">掛けた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>掛</rb><rt>か</rt></ruby>けた&nbsp;covered</span></span>。掛けるたびに真珠貝の裏に月の光が差した。</p>

<p>それから<span class="vocab" onclick="">星<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>星</rb><rt>ほし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;star</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">破片<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>破片</rb><rt>かけ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;splinter; heavens</span></span>を落ちている<span class="vocab" onclick="">間<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>間</rb><rt>ま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;period (of time)</span></span>に、<span class="vocab" onclick="">角<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>角</rb><rt>かど</rt></ruby>&nbsp;corners; edges</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">取れて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>取</rb><rt>と</rt></ruby>れて&nbsp;be taken off; be worn off</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">滑か<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>滑</rb><rt>なめら</rt></ruby>か&nbsp;smooth</span></span>になったんだろうと<span class="vocab" onclick="">思った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;thought; place</span></span>うちに、自分の<span class="vocab" onclick="">胸<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>胸</rb><rt>むね</rt></ruby>&nbsp;chest</span></span>と<span class="vocab" onclick="">手<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>手</rb><rt>て</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hands; arms</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">少し<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>少</rb><rt>すこ</rt></ruby>し&nbsp;a little; a bit</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">暖くなった<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>暖</rb><rt>あたたか</rt></ruby>くなった&nbsp;grew warm</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">苔<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>苔</rb><rt>こけ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;moss</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;top of</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">坐った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>坐</rb><rt>すわ</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;sat down</span></span>。これから<span class="vocab" onclick="">百年<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>百年</rb><rt>ひゃくねん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;a hundred years</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">間<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>間</rb><rt>あいだ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;period (of time)</span></span>こうして<span class="vocab" onclick="">待って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>待</rb><rt>ま</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;wait</span></span>いるんだなと<span class="vocab" onclick="">考えながら<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>考</rb><rt>かんが</rt></ruby>えながら&nbsp;thinking; considering</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">腕組をして<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>腕組</rb><rt>うでぐみ</rt></ruby>をして&nbsp;fold one's arms in front of one</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">丸い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>丸</rb><rt>まる</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;round</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">墓石<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>墓石</rb><rt>はかいし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;gravestone</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">眺めて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眺</rb><rt>なが</rt></ruby>めて&nbsp;gaze at</span></span>いた。そのうちに、<span class="vocab" onclick="">女<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>女</rb><rt>おんな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;woman</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">云った通り<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った<ruby><rb>通</rb><rt>とお</rt></ruby>り&nbsp;exactly as (she) said</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">日<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>日</rb><rt>ひ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;sun</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">東<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>東</rb><rt>ひがし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;east</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">出た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>で</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;appeared; descended</span></span>。赤いまんまでのっと<span class="vocab" onclick="">落ちて行った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>落</rb><rt>お</rt></ruby>ちて<ruby><rb>行</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;went down</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">一つ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>一</rb><rt>ひと</rt></ruby>つ&nbsp;one</span></span>と自分は<span class="vocab" onclick="">勘定した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>勘定</rb><rt>かんじょう</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;counted</span></span>。</p>

<p>しばらくするとまた<span class="vocab" onclick="">唐紅の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>唐紅</rb><rt>からくれない</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;crimson</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">天道<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>天道</rb><rt>てんとう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;the sun</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">のそりと<span class="vocabdef">のそりと&nbsp;heavily</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">上って来た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>のぼ</rt></ruby>って<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;rose; came up</span></span>。そうして<span class="vocab" onclick="">黙って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>黙</rb><rt>だま</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;in silence</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">沈んで<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>沈</rb><rt>しず</rt></ruby>んで&nbsp;sink; go down</span></span>しまった。<span class="vocab" onclick="">二つ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>二</rb><rt>ふた</rt></ruby>つ&nbsp;two</span></span>とまた勘定した。</p>

<p>自分は<span class="vocab" onclick="">こう云う風に<span class="vocabdef">こう<ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>う<ruby><rb>風</rb><rt>ふう</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;in this manner</span></span>一つ二つと勘定して行くうちに、赤い日をいくつ<span class="vocab" onclick="">見た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;saw; watched</span></span>か<span class="vocab" onclick="">分らない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>分</rb><rt>わか</rt></ruby>らない&nbsp;don't know</span></span>。勘定しても、勘定しても、<span class="vocab" onclick="">しつくせない<span class="vocabdef">しつくせない&nbsp;can't manage; can't keep up (with something)</span></span>ほど赤い日が<span class="vocab" onclick="">頭<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>頭</rb><rt>あたま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;head</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;above</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">通り越して行った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>通</rb><rt>とお</rt></ruby>り<ruby><rb>越</rb><rt>こ</rt></ruby>して<ruby><rb>行</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;passed by; went past</span></span>。それでも百年が<span class="vocab" onclick="">まだ来ない<span class="vocabdef">まだ<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>こ</rt></ruby>ない&nbsp;not yet arrive</span></span>。しまいには、苔の<span class="vocab" onclick="">生えた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>生</rb><rt>は</rt></ruby>えた&nbsp;grew (on)</span></span>丸い<span class="vocab" onclick="">石<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>石</rb><rt>いし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;stone</span></span>を眺めて、自分は女に<span class="vocab" onclick="">欺された<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>欺</rb><rt>だま</rt></ruby>された&nbsp;be deceived</span></span>のではなかろうかと<span class="vocab" onclick="">思い出した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>い<ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>だ</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;began to wonder</span></span>。</p>

<p>すると石の<span class="vocab" onclick="">下から<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>下</rb><rt>した</rt></ruby>から&nbsp;from below</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">斜に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>斜</rb><rt>はす</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;obliquely; at an angle</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">自分の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;one's own</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">方<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>方</rb><rt>ほう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;direction</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">向いて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>向</rb><rt>む</rt></ruby>いて&nbsp;turning (toward)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">青い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>青</rb><rt>あお</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;green</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">茎<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>茎</rb><rt>くき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;stem; stalk</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">伸びて来た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>伸</rb><rt>の</rt></ruby>びて<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;extended; stretched (toward one)</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">見る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;watch</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">間<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>間</rb><rt>ま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;period (of time)</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">長くなって<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>長</rb><rt>なが</rt></ruby>くなって&nbsp;lengthened</span></span>ちょうど自分の<span class="vocab" onclick="">胸<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>胸</rb><rt>むね</rt></ruby>&nbsp;chest</span></span>のあたりまで来て<span class="vocab" onclick="">留まった<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>留</rb><rt>と</rt></ruby>まった&nbsp;stopped</span></span>。と思うと、<span class="vocab" onclick="">すらりと<span class="vocabdef">すらりと&nbsp;smoothly; tip</span></span>に、<span class="vocab" onclick="">心持<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>心持</rb><rt>こころもち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;slightly; a shade</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">首<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>首</rb><rt>くび</rt></ruby>&nbsp;neck</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">傾けて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>傾</rb><rt>かたぶ</rt></ruby>けて&nbsp;incline; tilt</span></span>いた<span class="vocab" onclick="">細長い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>細長</rb><rt>ほそなが</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;slender</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">一輪<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>一輪</rb><rt>いちりん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;single (flower)</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">蕾<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>蕾</rb><rt>つぼみ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;(flower) bud</span></span>が、<span class="vocab" onclick="">ふっくらと<span class="vocabdef">ふっくらと&nbsp;amply; generously</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">弁<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>弁</rb><rt>はなびら</rt></ruby>&nbsp;flower petals (usually <ruby><rb>花弁</rb><rt>はなびら</rt></ruby>)</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">開いた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>開</rb><rt>ひら</rt></ruby>いた&nbsp;opened</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">真白な<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>真白</rb><rt>まっしろ</rt></ruby>な&nbsp;pure white</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">百合<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>百合</rb><rt>ゆり</rt></ruby>&nbsp;lily</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">鼻の先<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鼻</rb><rt>はな</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>先</rb><rt>さき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tip of one's nose</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">骨に徹える<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>骨</rb><rt>ほね</rt></ruby>に<ruby><rb>徹</rb><rt>こた</rt></ruby>える&nbsp;penetrate to the bone; shook</span></span>。自分は<span class="vocab" onclick="">首<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>首</rb><rt>くび</rt></ruby>&nbsp;neck; head</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">前<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>前</rb><rt>まえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;forward</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">出して<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>だ</rt></ruby>して&nbsp;put forth</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">冷たい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>冷</rb><rt>つめ</rt></ruby>たい&nbsp;cold</span></span>露の<span class="vocab" onclick="">滴る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>滴</rb><rt>したた</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;drip; reflexively</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">遠い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>遠</rb><rt>とお</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;far away; distant</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">空<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>空</rb><rt>そら</rt></ruby>&nbsp;sky</span></span>を見たら、<span class="vocab" onclick="">暁<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>暁</rb><rt>あかつき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;dawn; <p>「百年はもう来ていたんだな」とこの<span class="vocab" onclick="">時<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>時</rb><rt>とき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;time; moment</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">始めて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>始</rb><rt>はじ</rt></ruby>めて&nbsp;for the first time</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">気がついた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>気</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>がついた&nbsp;realized</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">第二<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>第二</rb><rt>だいに</rt></ruby>&nbsp;2nd</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">夜<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>夜</rb><rt>や</rt></ruby>&nbsp;night</span></span></p><br/>

<p>こんな<span class="vocab" onclick="">夢<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>夢</rb><rt>ゆめ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;dream</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">見た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;saw; had (a dream)</span></span></p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">和尚<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>和尚</rb><rt>おしょう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;(Buddhist) head priest</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">室<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>室</rb><rt>しつ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;room</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">退がって<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>退</rb><rt>さ</rt></ruby>がって&nbsp;withdraw from</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">廊下伝いに<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>廊下</rb><rt>ろうか</rt></ruby><ruby><rb>伝</rb><rt>づた</rt></ruby>いに&nbsp;following the corridor</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">自分の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;one's own; my own</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">部屋<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>部屋</rb><rt>へや</rt></ruby>&nbsp;room</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">帰る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>帰</rb><rt>かえ</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;return (to)</span></span>と<span class="vocab" onclick="">行灯<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>行灯</rb><rt>あんどう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;papered lantern</span></span>がぼんやり<span class="vocab" onclick="">点って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>点</rb><rt>とも</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;be lit; <p><span class="vocab" onclick="">襖<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>襖</rb><rt>ふすま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;fusuma (sliding screen with single covered surface, often decorated)</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">画<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>画</rb><rt>え</rt></ruby>&nbsp;painting</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">蕪村<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>蕪村</rb><rt>ぶそん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;Buson (Edo period poet and painter; be displayed (on a wall)</span></span>いる。<span class="vocab" onclick="">焚き残した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>焚</rb><rt>た</rt></ruby>き<ruby><rb>残</rb><rt>のこ</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;unburned; charred</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">線香<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>線香</rb><rt>せんこう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;incense</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">暗い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>暗</rb><rt>くら</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;dark</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">方<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>方</rb><rt>ほう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;direction; <p><span class="vocab" onclick="">立膝をした<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>立膝</rb><rt>たてひざ</rt></ruby>をした&nbsp;with one knee drawn up</span></span>まま、<span class="vocab" onclick="">左の手<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>左</rb><rt>ひだり</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>手</rb><rt>て</rt></ruby>&nbsp;left hand</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">座蒲団<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>座蒲団</rb><rt>ざぶとん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;seating cushion</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">捲って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>捲</rb><rt>めく</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;peel back; peel up</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">右<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>右</rb><rt>みぎ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;right (hand)</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">差し込んで<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>差</rb><rt>さ</rt></ruby>し<ruby><rb>込</rb><rt>こ</rt></ruby>んで&nbsp;insert; thrust into</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">見る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;(try and) see</span></span>と、<span class="vocab" onclick="">思った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;expected</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">所<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>所</rb><rt>ところ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;place</span></span>に、ちゃんとあった。あれば<span class="vocab" onclick="">安心<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>安心</rb><rt>あんしん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;reassurance; peace of mind</span></span>だから、<span class="vocab" onclick="">蒲団<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>蒲団</rb><rt>ふとん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;cushion</span></span>をもとのごとく<span class="vocab" onclick="">直して<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>直</rb><rt>なお</rt></ruby>して&nbsp;fix; straighten</span></span>、その<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;top</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">どっかり<span class="vocabdef">どっかり&nbsp;heavily; with a thud</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">坐った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>坐</rb><rt>すわ</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;sat down</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">お前<span class="vocabdef">お<ruby><rb>前</rb><rt>まえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;you (condescending)</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">侍<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>侍</rb><rt>さむらい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;samurai</span></span>である。侍なら<span class="vocab" onclick="">悟れぬ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>悟</rb><rt>さと</rt></ruby>れぬ&nbsp;can't attain enlightenment</span></span>はずはなかろうと<span class="vocab" onclick="">和尚<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>和尚</rb><rt>おしょう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;(Buddhist) head priest</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">云った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;said</span></span>。そういつまでも悟れぬところをもって見ると、<span class="vocab" onclick="">御前<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>御前</rb><rt>おまえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;you (condescending)</span></span>は侍ではあるまいと言った。<span class="vocab" onclick="">人間<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>人間</rb><rt>にんげん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;humanity</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">屑<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>屑</rb><rt>くず</rt></ruby>&nbsp;dregs</span></span>じゃと言った。ははあ<span class="vocab" onclick="">怒った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>怒</rb><rt>おこ</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;become angry</span></span>なと云って<span class="vocab" onclick="">笑った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>笑</rb><rt>わら</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;laughed</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">口惜しければ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>口惜</rb><rt>くや</rt></ruby>しければ&nbsp;be bothered; be chagrined</span></span>悟った<span class="vocab" onclick="">証拠<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>証拠</rb><rt>しょうこ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;evidence</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">持って来い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>持</rb><rt>も</rt></ruby>って<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>こ</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;bring; produce</span></span>と云って<span class="vocab" onclick="">ぷいと<span class="vocabdef">ぷいと&nbsp;quickly; abruptly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">向<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>向</rb><rt>むこう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;away; the other direction</span></span>をむいた。<span class="vocab" onclick="">怪しからん<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>怪</rb><rt>け</rt></ruby>しからん&nbsp;impertinent</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">隣の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>隣</rb><rt>となり</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;next door; adjacent</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">広間<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>広間</rb><rt>ひろま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hall</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">床<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>床</rb><rt>とこ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;alcove (short for <ruby><rb>床</rb><rt>とこ</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>間</rb><rt>ま</rt></ruby>)</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">据えて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>据</rb><rt>す</rt></ruby>えて&nbsp;set; fix (into position)</span></span>ある<span class="vocab" onclick="">置時計<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>置時計</rb><rt>おきどけい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;table clock</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">次<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>次</rb><rt>つぎ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;next</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">刻<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>刻</rb><rt>とき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hour</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">打つ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>打</rb><rt>う</rt></ruby>つ&nbsp;strike; chime (clock)</span></span>までには、きっと<span class="vocab" onclick="">悟って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>悟</rb><rt>さと</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;attain enlightenment</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">見せる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>せる&nbsp;show; demonstrate</span></span>。悟った<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;on top of; in addition to</span></span>で、<span class="vocab" onclick="">今夜<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>今夜</rb><rt>こんや</rt></ruby>&nbsp;this evening</span></span>また<span class="vocab" onclick="">入室する<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>入室</rb><rt>にゅうしつ</rt></ruby>する&nbsp;enter a room; enter the priest's room to be tested (Buddhism)</span></span>。そうして和尚の<span class="vocab" onclick="">首<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>首</rb><rt>くび</rt></ruby>&nbsp;neck; head</span></span>と悟りと<span class="vocab" onclick="">引替<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>引替</rb><rt>ひきかえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;exchange; trade</span></span>にしてやる。悟らなければ、和尚の<span class="vocab" onclick="">命<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>命</rb><rt>いのち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;life</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">取れない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>取</rb><rt>と</rt></ruby>れない&nbsp;cannot take</span></span>。どうしても悟らなければならない。<span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>は侍である。</p>

<p>もし悟れなければ<span class="vocab" onclick="">自刃<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自刃</rb><rt>じじん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;suicide by sword</span></span>する。<span class="vocab" onclick="">侍<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>侍</rb><rt>さむらい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;samurai</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">辱しめられて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>辱</rb><rt>はずか</rt></ruby>しめられて&nbsp;be shamed</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">生きて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>生</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>きて&nbsp;live</span></span>いる<span class="vocab" onclick="">訳には行かない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>訳</rb><rt>わけ</rt></ruby>には<ruby><rb>行</rb><rt>ゆ</rt></ruby>かない&nbsp;it won't do to ...; one can't ...</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">綺麗に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>綺麗</rb><rt>きれい</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;cleanly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">死んで<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>死</rb><rt>し</rt></ruby>んで&nbsp;die</span></span>しまう。</p>

<p>こう<span class="vocab" onclick="">考えた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>考</rb><rt>かんが</rt></ruby>えた&nbsp;reasoned; considered</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">時<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>時</rb><rt>とき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;time</span></span>、自分の<span class="vocab" onclick="">手<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>手</rb><rt>て</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hand</span></span>はまた<span class="vocab" onclick="">思わず<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>わず&nbsp;reflexively</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">布団<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>布団</rb><rt>ふとん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;cushion</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">下<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>下</rb><rt>した</rt></ruby>&nbsp;underside</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">這入った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>這入</rb><rt>はい</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;entered; reached into</span></span>。そうして<span class="vocab" onclick="">朱鞘<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>朱鞘</rb><rt>しゅざや</rt></ruby>&nbsp;red-lacquered sword sheath</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">短刀<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>短刀</rb><rt>たんとう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;short sword; dagger</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">引き摺り出した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>引</rb><rt>ひ</rt></ruby>き<ruby><rb>摺</rb><rt>ず</rt></ruby>り<ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>だ</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;dragged out; drew forth</span></span>。ぐっと<span class="vocab" onclick="">束<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>束</rb><rt>つか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hilt; haft</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">握って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>握</rb><rt>にぎ</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;grasp; grip</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">赤い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>赤</rb><rt>あか</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;red</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">鞘<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鞘</rb><rt>さや</rt></ruby>&nbsp;sheath</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">向へ払ったら<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>向</rb><rt>むこう</rt></ruby>へ<ruby><rb>払</rb><rt>はら</rt></ruby>ったら&nbsp;cast away</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">冷たい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>冷</rb><rt>つめ</rt></ruby>たい&nbsp;cold</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">刃<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>刃</rb><rt>は</rt></ruby>&nbsp;blade</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">一度に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>一度</rb><rt>いちど</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;at once; at the same time</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">暗い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>暗</rb><rt>くら</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;dark</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">部屋<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>部屋</rb><rt>へや</rt></ruby>&nbsp;room</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">光った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>光</rb><rt>ひか</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;glistened</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">凄い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>凄</rb><rt>すご</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;terrible; dreadful</span></span>ものが<span class="vocab" onclick="">手元<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>手元</rb><rt>てもと</rt></ruby>&nbsp;grip; handle</span></span>から、<span class="vocab" onclick="">すうすうと<span class="vocabdef">すうすうと&nbsp;with a hissing sound</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">逃げて行く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>逃</rb><rt>に</rt></ruby>げて<ruby><rb>行</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;escape</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">ように思われる<span class="vocabdef">ように<ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>われる&nbsp;it seemed that ...</span></span>。そうして、<span class="vocab" onclick="">ことごとく<span class="vocabdef">ことごとく&nbsp;fully; entirely</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">切先<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>切先</rb><rt>きっさき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;point; tip (of a blade)</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">集まって<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>集</rb><rt>あつ</rt></ruby>まって&nbsp;gathered; to one's dismay</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">針の頭<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>針</rb><rt>はり</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>頭</rb><rt>あたま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;head of a pin; head of a tack</span></span>のように<span class="vocab" onclick="">縮められて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>縮</rb><rt>ちぢ</rt></ruby>められて&nbsp;shrink; shorten</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">九寸五分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>九寸</rb><rt>くすん</rt></ruby><ruby><rb>五分</rb><rt>ごぶ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;dagger</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">先<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>先</rb><rt>さき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tip</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">来て<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>て&nbsp;come (to)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">やむをえず<span class="vocabdef">やむをえず&nbsp;unavoidably</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">尖って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>尖</rb><rt>とが</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;sharp; tapered</span></span>るのを<span class="vocab" onclick="">見て<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>て&nbsp;see; look at</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">たちまち<span class="vocabdef">たちまち&nbsp;suddenly; at once</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">ぐさりと<span class="vocabdef">ぐさりと&nbsp;with a thrust; plunging into</span></span>やりたくなった。<span class="vocab" onclick="">身体<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>身体</rb><rt>からだ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;body</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">血<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>血</rb><rt>ち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;blood</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">右の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>右</rb><rt>みぎ</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;right (side)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">手首<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>手首</rb><rt>てくび</rt></ruby>&nbsp;wrist</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">方<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>方</rb><rt>ほう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;direction</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">流れて来て<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>流</rb><rt>なが</rt></ruby>れて<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>て&nbsp;flowed into</span></span>、握っている<span class="vocab" onclick="">束<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>束</rb><rt>つか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hilt; haft</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">にちゃにちゃする<span class="vocabdef">にちゃにちゃする&nbsp;be sticky; be slimy</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">唇<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>唇</rb><rt>くちびる</rt></ruby>&nbsp;lips</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">顫えた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>顫</rb><rt>ふる</rt></ruby>えた&nbsp;trembled</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">短刀<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>短刀</rb><rt>たんとう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;short sword; dagger</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">鞘<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鞘</rb><rt>さや</rt></ruby>&nbsp;sheath</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">収めて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>収</rb><rt>おさ</rt></ruby>めて&nbsp;put away (in)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">右脇<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>右脇</rb><rt>みぎわき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;(one's) right side</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">引きつけて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>引</rb><rt>ひ</rt></ruby>きつけて&nbsp;keep close at hand</span></span>おいて、それから<span class="vocab" onclick="">全伽を組んだ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>全伽</rb><rt>ぜんが</rt></ruby>を<ruby><rb>組</rb><rt>く</rt></ruby>んだ&nbsp;assumed the lotus position (for meditation)</span></span>。――<span class="vocab" onclick="">趙州<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>趙州</rb><rt>じょうしゅう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;Jōshū Jūshin (Chinese Zen master; 778–897)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">曰く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>曰</rb><rt>いわ</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;according to ...</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">無<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>無</rb><rt>む</rt></ruby>&nbsp;nothingness</span></span>と。無とは<span class="vocab" onclick="">何<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>何</rb><rt>なん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;what</span></span>だ。<span class="vocab" onclick="">糞坊主め<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>糞坊主</rb><rt>くそぼうず</rt></ruby>め&nbsp;Damn that priest; Damn him (Jōshū) anyway</span></span>と<span class="vocab" onclick="">はがみをした<span class="vocabdef">はがみをした&nbsp;ground one's teeth (in anger)</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">奥歯<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>奥歯</rb><rt>おくば</rt></ruby>&nbsp;molars; back teeth</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">強く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>強</rb><rt>つよ</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;strongly; tightly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">咬み締めた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>咬</rb><rt>か</rt></ruby>み<ruby><rb>締</rb><rt>し</rt></ruby>めた&nbsp;clenched (teeth)</span></span>ので、<span class="vocab" onclick="">鼻<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鼻</rb><rt>はな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;nose; nostrils</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">熱い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>熱</rb><rt>あつ</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;hot</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">息<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>息</rb><rt>いき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;breath</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">荒く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>荒</rb><rt>あら</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;coarsely; unevenly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">出る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>で</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;emerge; come forth</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">こめかみ<span class="vocabdef">こめかみ&nbsp;temples (part of the body)</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">釣って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>釣</rb><rt>つ</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;cramp up (= <ruby><rb>痙</rb><rt>つ</rt></ruby>って)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">痛い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>痛</rb><rt>いた</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;be painful</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">眼<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眼</rb><rt>め</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eyes</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">普通<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>普通</rb><rt>ふつう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;usual</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">倍も<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>倍</rb><rt>ばい</rt></ruby>も&nbsp;double; twice as much</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">大きく開けて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>大</rb><rt>おお</rt></ruby>きく<ruby><rb>開</rb><rt>あ</rt></ruby>けて&nbsp;opened wide</span></span>やった。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">懸物<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>懸物</rb><rt>かけもの</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hanging picture (scroll)</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">見える<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>える&nbsp;be visible</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">行灯<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>行灯</rb><rt>あんどう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;papered lantern</span></span>が見える。<span class="vocab" onclick="">畳<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>畳</rb><rt>たたみ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tatami (mats)</span></span>が見える。<span class="vocab" onclick="">和尚<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>和尚</rb><rt>おしょう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;(Buddhist) head priest</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">薬缶頭<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>薬缶頭</rb><rt>やかんあたま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;bald head (lit: head like a copper kettle)</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">ありありと<span class="vocabdef">ありありと&nbsp;distinctly; vividly</span></span>見える。<span class="vocab" onclick="">鰐口<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鰐口</rb><rt>わにぐち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;big mouth (lit: alligator mouth)</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">開いて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>開</rb><rt>あ</rt></ruby>いて&nbsp;open</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">嘲笑った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>嘲笑</rb><rt>あざわら</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;sneered at; ridiculed</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">声<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>声</rb><rt>こえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;voice</span></span>まで<span class="vocab" onclick="">聞える<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>聞</rb><rt>きこ</rt></ruby>える&nbsp;could hear</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">怪しからん<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>怪</rb><rt>け</rt></ruby>しからん&nbsp;impertinent; insolent</span></span>坊主だ。どうしてもあの薬缶を<span class="vocab" onclick="">首にしなくてはならん<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>首</rb><rt>くび</rt></ruby>にしなくてはならん&nbsp;have to take his head</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">悟って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>悟</rb><rt>さと</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;attain enlightenment</span></span>やる。無だ、無だと<span class="vocab" onclick="">舌<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>舌</rb><rt>した</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tongue</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">根<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>根</rb><rt>ね</rt></ruby>&nbsp;base; root</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">念じた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>念</rb><rt>ねん</rt></ruby>じた&nbsp;chanted (an invocation)</span></span>。無だと<span class="vocab" onclick="">云う<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>う&nbsp;say; invoke</span></span>のにやっぱり<span class="vocab" onclick="">線香<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>線香</rb><rt>せんこう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;incense</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">香<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>香</rb><rt>におい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;smell; scent</span></span>がした。何だ線香のくせに。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>はいきなり<span class="vocab" onclick="">拳骨<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>拳骨</rb><rt>げんこつ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;fist</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">固めて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>固</rb><rt>かた</rt></ruby>めて&nbsp;tighten</span></span>自分の<span class="vocab" onclick="">頭<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>頭</rb><rt>あたま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;head</span></span>をいやと云うほど<span class="vocab" onclick="">擲った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>擲</rb><rt>なぐ</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;beat; struck</span></span>。そうして<span class="vocab" onclick="">奥歯<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>奥歯</rb><rt>おくば</rt></ruby>&nbsp;molars; back teeth</span></span>をぎりぎりと<span class="vocab" onclick="">噛んだ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>噛</rb><rt>か</rt></ruby>んだ&nbsp;bite; grind</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">両腋<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>両腋</rb><rt>りょうわき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;both armpits; under one's arms</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">汗<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>汗</rb><rt>あせ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;sweat</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">出る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>で</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;emerge; come forth</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">背中<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>背中</rb><rt>せなか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;back; spine</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">棒<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>棒</rb><rt>ぼう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;staff; rod</span></span>のようになった。<span class="vocab" onclick="">膝の接目<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>膝</rb><rt>ひざ</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>接目</rb><rt>つぎめ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;knee joints</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">急に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>急</rb><rt>きゅう</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;suddenly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">痛くなった<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>痛</rb><rt>いた</rt></ruby>くなった&nbsp;began to ache</span></span>。膝が<span class="vocab" onclick="">折れた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>折</rb><rt>お</rt></ruby>れた&nbsp;snap; fracture</span></span>ってどうあるものかと<span class="vocab" onclick="">思った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;thought; decided</span></span>。けれども痛い。<span class="vocab" onclick="">苦しい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>苦</rb><rt>くる</rt></ruby>しい&nbsp;intolerable; agonizing</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">無<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>無</rb><rt>む</rt></ruby>&nbsp;nothingness</span></span>はなかなか<span class="vocab" onclick="">出て来ない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>で</rt></ruby>て<ruby><rb>来</rb><rt>こ</rt></ruby>ない&nbsp;did not appear; did not arrive</span></span>。出て来ると思うとすぐ痛くなる。<span class="vocab" onclick="">腹が立つ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>腹</rb><rt>はら</rt></ruby>が<ruby><rb>立</rb><rt>た</rt></ruby>つ&nbsp;became angry</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">無念になる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>無念</rb><rt>むねん</rt></ruby>になる&nbsp;grew resentful</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">非常に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>非常</rb><rt>ひじょう</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;exceedingly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">口惜しくなる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>口惜</rb><rt>くや</rt></ruby>しくなる&nbsp;felt vexed (by failure)</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">涙<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>涙</rb><rt>なみだ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tears</span></span>がほろほろ出る。<span class="vocab" onclick="">ひと思に<span class="vocabdef">ひと<ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おもい</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;resolutely; once and for all</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">身<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>身</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>&nbsp;body</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">巨巌<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>巨巌</rb><rt>おおいわ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;giant boulder; large rock</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;top of</span></span>にぶつけて、<span class="vocab" onclick="">骨<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>骨</rb><rt>ほね</rt></ruby>&nbsp;bones</span></span>も<span class="vocab" onclick="">肉<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>肉</rb><rt>にく</rt></ruby>&nbsp;flesh</span></span>もめちゃめちゃに<span class="vocab" onclick="">砕いて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>砕</rb><rt>くだ</rt></ruby>いて&nbsp;smash; break (into pieces)</span></span>しまいたくなる。</p>

<p>それでも<span class="vocab" onclick="">我慢して<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>我慢</rb><rt>がまん</rt></ruby>して&nbsp;persevere; exercise self control</span></span>じっと<span class="vocab" onclick="">坐って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>坐</rb><rt>すわ</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;sit</span></span>いた。<span class="vocab" onclick="">堪えがたい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>堪</rb><rt>た</rt></ruby>えがたい&nbsp;intolerable; unbearable</span></span>ほど<span class="vocab" onclick="">切ない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>切</rb><rt>せつ</rt></ruby>ない&nbsp;oppressive; heartrending</span></span>ものを<span class="vocab" onclick="">胸<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>胸</rb><rt>むね</rt></ruby>&nbsp;breast; bosom</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">盛れて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>盛</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>れて&nbsp;put into; fill with</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">忍んで<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>忍</rb><rt>しの</rt></ruby>んで&nbsp;endure</span></span>いた。その切ないものが<span class="vocab" onclick="">身体中<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>身体中</rb><rt>からだじゅう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;throughout one's body</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">筋肉<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>筋肉</rb><rt>きんにく</rt></ruby>&nbsp;muscle; sinew</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">下<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>下</rb><rt>した</rt></ruby>&nbsp;below; beneath</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">持上げて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>持上</rb><rt>もちあ</rt></ruby>げて&nbsp;lift up</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">毛穴<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>毛穴</rb><rt>けあな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;pores (of the skin)</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">外<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>外</rb><rt>そと</rt></ruby>&nbsp;outward</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">吹き出よう<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>吹</rb><rt>ふ</rt></ruby>き<ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>で</rt></ruby>よう&nbsp;break out</span></span>吹き出ようと<span class="vocab" onclick="">焦る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>焦</rb><rt>あせ</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;be impatient</span></span>けれども、どこも<span class="vocab" onclick="">一面<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>一面</rb><rt>いちめん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;the whole surface</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">塞がって<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>塞</rb><rt>ふさ</rt></ruby>がって&nbsp;be blocked; be clogged</span></span>、まるで<span class="vocab" onclick="">出口<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>出口</rb><rt>でぐち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;exit; way out</span></span>がないような<span class="vocab" onclick="">残刻<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>残刻</rb><rt>ざんこく</rt></ruby>&nbsp;cruelty (usually <ruby><rb>残酷</rb><rt>ざんこく</rt></ruby>)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">極まる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>極</rb><rt>きわ</rt></ruby>まる&nbsp;the height of; the extreme of</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">状態<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>状態</rb><rt>じょうたい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;condition; state</span></span>であった。</p>

<p>そのうちに<span class="vocab" onclick="">頭が変になった<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>頭</rb><rt>あたま</rt></ruby>が<ruby><rb>変</rb><rt>へん</rt></ruby>になった&nbsp;lost one's mind; came unhinged</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">行灯<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>行灯</rb><rt>あんどう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;papered lantern</span></span>も<span class="vocab" onclick="">蕪村<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>蕪村</rb><rt>ぶそん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;Buson (Edo period poet and painter; 1716-1784)</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">画<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>画</rb><rt>え</rt></ruby>&nbsp;painting</span></span>も、<span class="vocab" onclick="">畳<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>畳</rb><rt>たたみ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tatami (mats)</span></span>も、<span class="vocab" onclick="">違棚<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>違棚</rb><rt>ちがいだな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;staggered shelves</span></span>も<span class="vocab" onclick="">有って無い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>有</rb><rt>あ</rt></ruby>って<ruby><rb>無</rb><rt>な</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;there but not there</span></span>ような、無くって有るように<span class="vocab" onclick="">見えた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>えた&nbsp;appeared</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">と云って<span class="vocabdef">と<ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;even so; nevertheless</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">無<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>無</rb><rt>む</rt></ruby>&nbsp;nothingness</span></span>はちっとも<span class="vocab" onclick="">現前しない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>現前</rb><rt>げんぜん</rt></ruby>しない&nbsp;did not appear</span></span>。ただ<span class="vocab" onclick="">好加減に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>好加減</rb><rt>いいかげん</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;halfheartedly; perfunctorily</span></span>坐っていたようである。ところへ<span class="vocab" onclick="">忽然<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>忽然</rb><rt>こつぜん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;suddenly; abruptly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">隣<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>隣</rb><rt>となり</rt></ruby>&nbsp;neighboring</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">座敷<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>座敷</rb><rt>ざしき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;hall</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">時計<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>時計</rb><rt>とけい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;clock</span></span>がチーンと<span class="vocab" onclick="">鳴り始めた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鳴</rb><rt>な</rt></ruby>り<ruby><rb>始</rb><rt>はじ</rt></ruby>めた&nbsp;began to chime</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">はっと思った<span class="vocabdef">はっと<ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;was caught by surprise</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">右の手<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>右</rb><rt>みぎ</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>手</rb><rt>て</rt></ruby>&nbsp;right hand</span></span>をすぐ<span class="vocab" onclick="">短刀<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>短刀</rb><rt>たんとう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;short sword; dagger</span></span>にかけた。時計が<span class="vocab" onclick="">二つ目<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>二</rb><rt>ふた</rt></ruby>つ<ruby><rb>目</rb><rt>め</rt></ruby>&nbsp;second one; (for the) second time</span></span>をチーンと<span class="vocab" onclick="">打った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>打</rb><rt>う</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;struck; chimed</span></span>。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">第三<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>第三</rb><rt>だいさん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;3rd</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">夜<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>夜</rb><rt>や</rt></ruby>&nbsp;night</span></span></p><br/>

<p>こんな<span class="vocab" onclick="">夢<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>夢</rb><rt>ゆめ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;dream</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">見た<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>た&nbsp;saw; had (a dream)</span></span></p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">六つ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>六</rb><rt>むっ</rt></ruby>つ&nbsp;six (years old)</span></span>になる<span class="vocab" onclick="">子供<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>子供</rb><rt>こども</rt></ruby>&nbsp;child</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">負って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>負</rb><rt>おぶ</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;carry (a baby or child) on one's back</span></span>る。たしかに<span class="vocab" onclick="">自分の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;one's own; my own</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">子<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>子</rb><rt>こ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;child</span></span>である。ただ<span class="vocab" onclick="">不思議な<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>不思議</rb><rt>ふしぎ</rt></ruby>な&nbsp;strange; curious</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">事<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>事</rb><rt>こと</rt></ruby>&nbsp;fact; matter; affair</span></span>には<span class="vocab" onclick="">いつの間にか<span class="vocabdef">いつの<ruby><rb>間</rb><rt>ま</rt></ruby>にか&nbsp;before one knows it</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">眼が潰れて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眼</rb><rt>め</rt></ruby>が<ruby><rb>潰</rb><rt>つぶ</rt></ruby>れて&nbsp;be blind</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">青坊主<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>青坊主</rb><rt>あおぼうず</rt></ruby>&nbsp;person with a shaved head</span></span>になっている。<span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">御前の<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>御前</rb><rt>おまえ</rt></ruby>の&nbsp;your</span></span>眼はいつ潰れたのかいと<span class="vocab" onclick="">聞く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>聞</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;ask</span></span>と、なに<span class="vocab" onclick="">昔<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>昔</rb><rt>むかし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;long ago</span></span>からさと<span class="vocab" onclick="">答えた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>答</rb><rt>こた</rt></ruby>えた&nbsp;answered</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">声<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>声</rb><rt>こえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;voice</span></span>は子供の声<span class="vocab" onclick="">に相違ない<span class="vocabdef">に<ruby><rb>相違</rb><rt>そうい</rt></ruby>ない&nbsp;without a doubt</span></span>が、<span class="vocab" onclick="">言葉つき<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>言葉</rb><rt>ことば</rt></ruby>つき&nbsp;diction; manner of speaking</span></span>はまるで<span class="vocab" onclick="">大人<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>大人</rb><rt>おとな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;adult</span></span>である。しかも<span class="vocab" onclick="">対等<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>対等</rb><rt>たいとう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;on even terms; not deferential</span></span>だ。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">左右<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>左右</rb><rt>さゆう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;left and right; both sides</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">青田<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>青田</rb><rt>あおた</rt></ruby>&nbsp;green rice paddies</span></span>である。<span class="vocab" onclick="">路<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>路</rb><rt>みち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;path; way</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">細い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>細</rb><rt>ほそ</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;narrow</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">鷺<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鷺</rb><rt>さぎ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;snowy heron; egret</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">影<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>影</rb><rt>かげ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;shape; form</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">時々<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>時々</rb><rt>ときどき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;sometimes; on occasion</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">闇<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>闇</rb><rt>やみ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;the dark; darkness</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">差す<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>差</rb><rt>さ</rt></ruby>す&nbsp;shine; flash</span></span>。</p>

<p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">田圃<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>田圃</rb><rt>たんぼ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;paddies; rice fields</span></span>へかかったね」と<span class="vocab" onclick="">背中<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>背中</rb><rt>せなか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;back (body)</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">云った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;said; remarked</span></span>。</p>

<p>「どうして<span class="vocab" onclick="">解る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>解</rb><rt>わか</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;understand; know</span></span>」と<span class="vocab" onclick="">顔<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>顔</rb><rt>かお</rt></ruby>&nbsp;face</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">後ろへ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>後</rb><rt>うし</rt></ruby>ろへ&nbsp;toward the rear; behind</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">振り向ける<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>振</rb><rt>ふ</rt></ruby>り<ruby><rb>向</rb><rt>む</rt></ruby>ける&nbsp;turn (to look) back</span></span>ようにして聞いたら、</p>

<p>「だって鷺が<span class="vocab" onclick="">鳴く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鳴</rb><rt>な</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;cry; call (birds)</span></span>じゃないか」と答えた。</p>

<p>すると鷺がはたして<span class="vocab" onclick="">二声<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>二声</rb><rt>ふたこえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;two cries; two calls</span></span>ほど鳴いた。</p>

<p>自分は<span class="vocab" onclick="">我子<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>我子</rb><rt>わがこ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;one's own child</span></span>ながら<span class="vocab" onclick="">少し<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>少</rb><rt>すこ</rt></ruby>し&nbsp;a little; a bit</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">怖くなった<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>怖</rb><rt>こわ</rt></ruby>くなった&nbsp;became fearful</span></span>。こんなものを<span class="vocab" onclick="">背負って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>背負</rb><rt>しょ</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;carry on one's back; be saddled with</span></span>いては、<span class="vocab" onclick="">この先<span class="vocabdef">この<ruby><rb>先</rb><rt>さき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;after this; from now</span></span>どうなるか<span class="vocab" onclick="">分らない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>分</rb><rt>わか</rt></ruby>らない&nbsp;don't know; can't tell</span></span>。どこか<span class="vocab" onclick="">打遣ゃる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>打遣</rb><rt>うっち</rt></ruby>ゃる&nbsp;cast away; abandon</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">所<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>所</rb><rt>ところ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;place</span></span>はなかろうかと<span class="vocab" onclick="">向う<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>向</rb><rt>むこ</rt></ruby>う&nbsp;the distance; ahead</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">見る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;look (toward)</span></span>と<span class="vocab" onclick="">闇の中<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>闇</rb><rt>やみ</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>中</rb><rt>なか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;in the darkness</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">大きな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>大</rb><rt>おお</rt></ruby>きな&nbsp;large; thick</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">森<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>森</rb><rt>もり</rt></ruby>&nbsp;woods</span></span>が見えた。あすこならばと<span class="vocab" onclick="">考え出す<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>考</rb><rt>かんが</rt></ruby>え<ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>だ</rt></ruby>す&nbsp;conclude; settle on</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">途端<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>途端</rb><rt>とたん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;moment; instant</span></span>に、背中で、</p>

<p>「ふふん」と云う声がした。</p>

<p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">何<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>何</rb><rt>なに</rt></ruby>&nbsp;what</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">笑う<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>笑</rb><rt>わら</rt></ruby>う&nbsp;laugh (about)</span></span>んだ」</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">子供<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>子供</rb><rt>こども</rt></ruby>&nbsp;child</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">返事<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>返事</rb><rt>へんじ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;answer</span></span>をしなかった。ただ</p>

<p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">御父さん<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>御父</rb><rt>おとっ</rt></ruby>さん&nbsp;father</span></span>、<span class="vocab" onclick="">重いかい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>重</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>いかい&nbsp;am I heavy</span></span>」と<span class="vocab" onclick="">聞いた<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>聞</rb><rt>き</rt></ruby>いた&nbsp;asked</span></span>。</p>

<p>「重かあない」と答えると</p>

<p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">今に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>今</rb><rt>いま</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;soon</span></span>重くなるよ」と云った。</p>

<p><span class="vocab" onclick="">自分<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;oneself; I</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">黙って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>黙</rb><rt>だま</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;in silence; midst</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">路<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>路</rb><rt>みち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;path; way</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">不規則に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>不規則</rb><rt>ふきそく</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;irregularly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">うねって<span class="vocabdef">うねって&nbsp;wind; meander</span></span>なかなか<span class="vocab" onclick="">思うように<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>うように&nbsp;as one hopes</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">出られない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>出</rb><rt>で</rt></ruby>られない&nbsp;couldn't emerge from</span></span>。しばらくすると<span class="vocab" onclick="">二股<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>二股</rb><rt>ふたまた</rt></ruby>&nbsp;fork; branch (road)</span></span>になった。自分は<span class="vocab" onclick="">股の根<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>股</rb><rt>また</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>根</rb><rt>ね</rt></ruby>&nbsp;base of the fork; junction point</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">立って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>立</rb><rt>た</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;stand; <p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">石<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>石</rb><rt>いし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;stone</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">立ってる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>立</rb><rt>た</rt></ruby>ってる&nbsp;stand; be erected</span></span>はずだがな」と<span class="vocab" onclick="">小僧<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>小僧</rb><rt>こぞう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;youngster</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">云った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;said</span></span>。</p>

<p>なるほど<span class="vocab" onclick="">八寸角<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>八寸角</rb><rt>はっすんかく</rt></ruby>&nbsp;8 sun (about 24 cm; about 10 inches) square</span></span>の石が<span class="vocab" onclick="">腰<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>腰</rb><rt>こし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;waist; <p>「左が<span class="vocab" onclick="">好い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>好</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;good; a better choice</span></span>だろう」と<span class="vocab" onclick="">小僧<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>小僧</rb><rt>こぞう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;youngster</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">命令した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>命令</rb><rt>めいれい</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;directed; instructed</span></span>。左を見るとさっきの森が<span class="vocab" onclick="">闇の影<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>闇</rb><rt>やみ</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>影</rb><rt>かげ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;shadow of darkness</span></span>を、<span class="vocab" onclick="">高い<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>高</rb><rt>たか</rt></ruby>い&nbsp;high; lofty</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">空<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>空</rb><rt>そら</rt></ruby>&nbsp;sky</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">自分らの<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>自分</rb><rt>じぶん</rt></ruby>らの&nbsp;our</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">頭<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>頭</rb><rt>あたま</rt></ruby>&nbsp;heads</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;above</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">抛げかけて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>抛</rb><rt>な</rt></ruby>げかけて&nbsp;throw over</span></span>いた。自分はちょっと<span class="vocab" onclick="">躊躇した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>躊躇</rb><rt>ちゅうちょ</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;hesitated</span></span>。</p>

<p>「<span class="vocab" onclick="">遠慮しないでもいい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>遠慮</rb><rt>えんりょ</rt></ruby>しないでもいい&nbsp;there's no need to hesitate; don't be afraid</span></span>」と小僧がまた<span class="vocab" onclick="">云った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;spoke</span></span>。自分は<span class="vocab" onclick="">仕方なしに<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>仕方</rb><rt>しかた</rt></ruby>なしに&nbsp;having no choice;
